[2:12:29] Isadank: Best of 3 can end on {3 or 2}; best of five can end on {3, 4, 5} However the set of numbers is always {games played}. So a so-called "Weighted Best of Five" would not have the end possibilities of a Non-weighted Bof5 ( {3,4,5} ) and would instead have the end possibilities {3,4} Thus it should be called a best of 4.
